<!-- logid field is 10 digits: First two: Log Type, Second Two: Subtype, Last 6: message id -->
<!-- currently we only match last 5 digits for log message id, but we should consider matching all 6 -->
<collectFieldsByRegex src="$logID">
<!-- We only chop off the leading 0 of the message id 6 digits -->
<regex><![CDATA[^\D*<_typeId:patTwoDigits><_catId:patTwoDigits>0?<_id:gPatInt>\D*$]]></regex>
</collectFieldsByRegex>

<when test="exist sentDeltaBytes64">
<when test="exist recvDeltaBytes64">
<setEventAttribute attr="totDeltaBytes64">add($sentDeltaBytes64, $recvDeltaBytes64)</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
<when test="not_private_ip destIpAddr">
<when test="exist destName">
<setEventAttribute attr="domainEntropy">calcDomainEntropy($destName)</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
<choose>
<when test="not_exist _severity"/>
<!-- debug, info, information, unknown: 1 -->
<when test="$_severity IN 'debug,information,info'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">1</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_severity = 'notice'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">3</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_severity = 'warning'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">5</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_severity IN 'error'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">7</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_severity = 'critical'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">9</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_severity = 'alert'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">10</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_severity = 'emergency'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">10</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</choose>
<!-- IPS -->
<setEventAttribute attr="_ips">0</setEventAttribute>
<when test="exist subtype">
<when test="$subtype = 'ips'">
<setEventAttribute attr="_ips">1</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
<when test="exist _type">
<when test="$_type = 'ips'">
<setEventAttribute attr="_ips">1</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
<when test="$_ips = '1'">
<choose>
<when test="$_ipssev IN 'info, low'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">3</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_ipssev = 'medium'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">7</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_ipssev = 'high'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">9</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$_ipssev = 'critical'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">10</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</choose>
<when test="exist _action">
<when test="$_action IN 'blocked, denied, deny, dropped'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventSeverity">7</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
</when>
<when test="not_exist infoURL">
<when test="exist uriStem">
<when test="matches($uriStem, '.://.')">
<setEventAttribute attr="infoURL">$uriStem</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
</when>
<when test="exist _hostName">
<switch>
<case>
<collectFieldsByRegex src="$_hostName">
<regex><![CDATA[^N/A$]]></regex>
</collectFieldsByRegex>
</case>
<case>
<collectFieldsByRegex src="$_hostName">
<regex><![CDATA[://<hostName:gPatHostName>]]></regex>
</collectFieldsByRegex>
<choose>
<when test="exist infoURL"/>
<when test="exist uriStem">
<setEventAttribute attr="infoURL">combineMsgId($_hostName, $uriStem)</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<otherwise>
<setEventAttribute attr="infoURL">$_hostName</setEventAttribute>
</otherwise>
</choose>
<when test="not_exist destName">
<setEventAttribute attr="destName">$hostName</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</case>
<case>
<collectFieldsByRegex src="$_hostName">
<regex><![CDATA[^<hostName:gPatHostName>$]]></regex>
</collectFieldsByRegex>
<when test="not_exist destName">
<setEventAttribute attr="destName">$_hostName</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</case>
<default/>
</switch>
</when>
<when test="not_exist infoURL">
<when test="exist hostName">
<when test="exist uriStem">
<choose>
<when test="not_exist serviceName"/>
<when test="$serviceName = 'HTTP'">
<setEventAttribute attr="infoURL">combineMsgId("http://", $hostName, $uriStem)</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<when test="$serviceName = 'HTTPS'">
<setEventAttribute attr="infoURL">combineMsgId("https://", $hostName, $uriStem)</setEventAttribute>
</when>
<otherwise>
<setEventAttribute attr="infoURL">combineMsgId($serviceName, "://", $hostName, $uriStem)</setEventAttribute>
</otherwise>
</choose>
</when>
</when>
</when>
<when test="not_exist eventAction">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventAction">0</setEventAttribute>
<choose>
<when test="exist _action">
<when test="$_action IN 'block, blocked, deny, dropped, ban-ip'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventAction">1</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
<when test="exist fwAction">
<when test="$fwAction IN 'block, blocked, deny, dropped, ban-ip'">
<setEventAttribute attr="eventAction">1</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
</choose>
</when>
<when test="exist _action">
<when test="not_exist fwAction">
<setEventAttribute attr="fwAction">$_action</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
<when test="not_exist srcIpAddr">
<!-- for admin action events parse source from ui= field -->
<when test="exist _ui">
<switch>
<case>
<collectFieldsByRegex src="$_ui">
<regex><![CDATA[^<authenMethod:gPatWord>\(<srcIpAddr:gPatIpAddr>\)$]]></regex>
</collectFieldsByRegex>
</case>
<default/>
</switch>
</when>
</when>
<when test="not_exist user">
<when test="exist _adminName">
<setEventAttribute attr="user">$_adminName</setEventAttribute>
</when>
</when>
</parsingInstructions>
